<p align=right style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-right:0pt;text-align:right;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">EXHIBIT

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-right:0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-right:0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-right:0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-right:0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-right:0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">The CATO
Corporation</font></b></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="border:none;"><font face=Courier lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><u><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:16.0pt;">NEWS
RELEASE</font></u></b></font></p>

<h1 style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="font-size:14.0pt;text-decoration:none;">&nbsp;</font></b></font></h1>

<h1 style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><u><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="font-size:14.0pt;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></u></b></font></h1>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;margin-left:1.5in;text-indent:.5in;"><font style="border:none;"><font face=Courier lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; &nbsp;</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">For Further Information Contact:</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; John R. Howe</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Executive Vice President</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Chief Financial Officer</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; 704-551-7315</font></font></p>

<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></font></p>

<div style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.5pt;padding:31.0pt 31.0pt 1.0pt 31.0pt;">

<p align=center style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;padding:0in;text-align:center;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:14.0pt;">CATO REPORTS 1Q NET LOSS</font></b></font></p>

</div>


<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-align:justify;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;font-weight:normal;letter-spacing:-.15pt;line-height:150%;">&nbsp;</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">CHARLOTTE, N.C. (May 21,
2020) &#8211;&#8211; </font></font><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">The Cato Corporation (NYSE: CATO) today reported net loss of $28.4
million or ($1.19) per diluted share for the first quarter ended May 2, 2020,
compared to net income of $21.3 million or $.87 per diluted share for the first
quarter ended May 4, 2019.&#160; Sales for the first quarter were $98.8 million, or
a decrease of 57% from sales of $228.1 million for the first quarter ended May
4, 2019.&#160;&#160; The Company&#8217;s same-store sales for the quarter decreased 56% to last
year.</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">&#8220;With the
health and safety of our associates and customers in mind, Cato closed its
stores on March 19th, along with most non-essential retailers.&#160; We were able to
reopen approximately 700 of our 1,300 stores May 1st and hope to have the rest
reopened by early June,&#8221; stated John Cato, Chairman, President, and Chief
Executive Officer.&#160; &#8220;As noted in recent business updates in regards to the
coronavirus pandemic, Cato has had to make difficult decisions in an effort to
sustain our business and safeguard the long-term health of our company by
cutting costs across the organization, preserving cash by reducing capital
expenditures, delaying or cancelling non-leased, planned new store development
and suspending the quarterly dividend.&#8221; </font></font></p>


<DIV bclFooter>


<p style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-border-shadow:yes;mso-padding-alt:31.0pt 31.0pt 31.0pt 31.0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;mso-bidi-font-family:Times New Roman;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;">8100 Denmark Road</font></font></p>

Box 34216</font></font></p>

<DIV bclHeader>


<p align=right style="border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:.0001pt;mso-border-shadow:yes;mso-padding-alt:31.0pt 31.0pt 31.0pt 31.0pt;tab-stops:center 3.0in right 6.0in;text-align:right;"><b><font style="mso-bidi-font-weight:normal;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;mso-bidi-font-family:Times New Roman;"><font style="mso-tab-count:1;"><b><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; &nbsp;</font></b></font></font></font></b></p>


</DIV>
<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">Gross margin decreased 24.9% to 15.4% of sales in the quarter, due
to a reduction in merchandise contribution, combined with the effects of
deleveraging resulting from the sales decline related to the store closures.&#160;
SG&amp;A expenses as a percent of sales increased 24.2% to 53.1% during the
quarter primarily due to the effects of deleveraging, and a store impairment
charge of $5.3 million, partially offset by reduced incentive compensation.&#160; A
pre-tax loss, coupled with the beneficial effects of the CARES Act has resulted
in a $9.1 million tax benefit versus a $4.3 million expense in the prior year.&#160;
The Company ended the quarter with unrestricted cash and short-term investments
of $147.8 million, including $30 million drawn on its revolving line of credit.</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">During the
first quarter ended May 2, 2020, the Company opened 24 new stores and
permanently closed 5 stores.&#160; At the time of this press release, the Company
has reopened approximately 1,175 stores in compliance with state and local
health and safety guidelines, with the remainder expected to be reopened by
early June.&#160; As of May 2, 2020, the Company has 1,300 stores in 31 states,
compared to 1,302 stores in 31 states as of May 4, 2019.</font></font></p>

<p style="background:white;border:none;margin:0in;margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;margin-top:12.0pt;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif style="border:none;"><font face=Arial,sans-serif lang=EN-US style="font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;">The Cato
Corporation is a leading specialty retailer of value-priced fashion apparel and
accessories operating three concepts, &#8220;Cato,&#8221; &#8220;Versona&#8221; and &#8220;It&#8217;s Fashion.&#8221;&#160;
The Company&#8217;s Cato stores offer exclusive merchandise with fashion and quality
comparable to mall specialty stores at low prices every day.&#160; The Company also
offers exclusive merchandise found in its Cato stores at www.catofashions.com.&#160;
Versona is a unique fashion destination offering apparel and accessories
including jewelry, handbags and shoes at exceptional prices every day.&#160; Select
Versona merchandise can also be found at www.shopversona.com.&#160; It&#8217;s Fashion
offers fashion with a focus on the latest trendy styles for the entire family
at low prices every day.</font></font></p>
